561. [Integrate] Random integrate trig 1148: sin2cos2 [format fuzz] [integrate_trig:sin2cos2]
================================================================================
Input:
1

3

Check:
check; calculated answer correctness; random input formatting fuzzed

Output:
1 int
2 de
3 param area
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
Met 1/2 n/p: Method: Integration by substitution
1. u = 4*x - 1/3*pi
2. du/dx = 4
3. du = 4 dx
4. I = Int[1/4*sin(u)^2*cos(u)^2] du
5. = -1/32*sin(4*u) + 1/8*u + C
6. Substitute back u = 4*x - 1/3*pi.
7. = -1/32*sin(4*(4*x - 1/3*pi)) + 1/8*(4*x - 1/3*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(16*x - 4/3*pi) + 1/2*x - 1/24*pi + C

7. = -1/128*sin(4*(3*x + 1/4*pi)) + 1/1024*sin(8*(3*x + 1/4*pi)) + 3/128*(3*x + 1/4*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/128*sin(12*x + pi) + 1/1024*sin(24*x + 2*pi) + 9/128*x + 3/512*pi + C
